msg:Yancheng Tianmu Hot Spring Resort Hotel
Location: Close to the Dutch Flower Sea, it is very convenient to drive by car. It will be there in a short time after getting off the highway. Parking is free
Environment: The hotel decoration is very new and the design style is quite fashionable. The switches in the room are all smart central controls and smart toilets. The room was very warm, but the soundproofing was not very good, and the sound from the corridor could be heard clearly. Both rooms have balconies, and we happened to see the sunset when we checked in. The sunset was beautiful. It‚Äôs definitely more beautiful when the weather is warm
Service: We booked 2 double-bed rooms. Because we had a baby, the front desk helped to upgrade 1 parent-child room for free. The experience was up up! There are staff to guide you throughout the check-in process. The front desk staff, Bian Jinnan and Li Zhoubin, are particularly proactive and enthusiastic. There are also welcome fruits in the room. Thank you!
Facilities: There is a gym on the 5th floor. It is quite big and there are not many people. There is an indoor playground for children on the second floor. Children as young as 3 years old can have a lot of fun with the ocean ball pool and slide. The key is that there are not many people and the experience is great
Child-friendly: The parent-child rooms are very uniquely decorated. We experienced the princess room, which was pink and tender and dreamy. The little girl Dajuliang liked it very much. There are children's toiletries, children's slippers, and sink footrests, which is very convenient for bringing children. The wardrobe is equipped with bathrobes for adults and children, as well as umbrellas, which is quite considerate.
Hot spring: When I checked in in the afternoon, the front desk said that the hot spring facilities were under maintenance and were not open for the time being. Later after dinner, I received a call from the hotel saying that they were open and you could try it for free. But I didn‚Äôt bring a swimsuit this time and I was in a hurry, so I didn‚Äôt go. I‚Äôll try it again next time I have a chance.
Breakfast: There are quite a variety of dishes, both Chinese and Western. I‚Äôm not used to eating noodles. My favorite is cheese + melon seeds hahaha
